Our catalog with **#20251018** (Catalog version **3.4.438** ) is available to our **Easy2Patch** customers.

This week, **99** software updates are provided in the E2P catalog. We support **543** products of **331** individual manufacturers in total. We are updating **712** products with 32/64-bit and language options.

***Note:*** *VirusTotal and Kaspersky Opentip scans are the responsibility of the manufacturer. E2P Bilisim has no responsibility or liability for the virus scanning results of the files.*

> V2.3.0 Public Release New Features Skip Part also skips unnecessary color-change flush Previously, when skipping a single part, only that part’s geometry was skipped; material change flush related to that part still occurred. With this change, color-change flush and waste-tower paths associated with the skipped part will also be omitted, effectively shortening print time and reducing material waste. This feature is currently supported on H2S and P2S.

> 5.5.243 Latest 💾 Save States: introducing ready-to-use, flexible "Save & Load" actions The new "Save State" actions allow to save & load an entire game - or some part of it - using only a few actions. By default, the save and load actions will save the full state of your game at any time — including all objects, variables, sounds, effects, and more. Saves can either be handled by GDevelop (which will save it on the device internal storage using the name you specify) or stored in a variable, giving you full control on where you store the content of this variable.

> Stable Channel Update for Desktop Tuesday, October 14, 2025 The Stable channel has been updated to 141.0.7390.107/.108 for Windows and Mac and 141.0.7390.107 for Linux, which will roll out over the coming days/weeks. A full list of changes in this build is available in the Log. Security Fixes and Rewards Note: Access to bug details and links may be kept restricted until a majority of users are updated with a fix. > Netpas Message “Your Communication Beyond eMail” Netpas Message is a maritime-focused email system designed to enhance message efficiency while maintaining the core functionalities of a traditional email program. It analyzes vessel data from incoming emails, stores it in the Vessel Manager database, and enables circulation via Open Tonnage.
